if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php') != 'f8fe29140160fbdca75a89cdec496983586dfa51') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php') !== 'f8fe29140160fbdca75a89cdec496983586dfa51') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php') !== 'be5d1b5a8df80f7e839d06f80d7f676919bb543d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php') !== 'f8fe29140160fbdca75a89cdec496983586dfa51') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/adminPages/401_backup/restore_backup.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '5b3fbf7e7471ad7acb9069b31eeface8ab466c32') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '5b3fbf7e7471ad7acb9069b31eeface8ab466c32') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '1411638987de675af965f73e8bc983c1553dfc9c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '5b3fbf7e7471ad7acb9069b31eeface8ab466c32') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
